CAR_great_game = {
	CAR_great_game_testing = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
		complete_effect = {
			INC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					log = "[state.GetID]"
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 0
	}
	CAR_great_game_royal_audience_of_auraucania_patagonia = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 270
				state = 507
				state = 512
				state = 579
				state = 1029
			}
			highlight_color_while_active = 3
			highlight_color_before_active = 2
		}
		allowed = {
			tag = CAR
		}
		visible = {
		}
		available = {
			AND = {
				AND = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = FOP
						}
						FOP = {
							is_subject_of = CAR
						}
					}
					FOP = {
						270 = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = CAR
									is_subject_of = CAR
								}
							}
						}
						507 = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = CAR
									is_subject_of = CAR
								}
							}
						}
						512 = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = CAR
									is_subject_of = CAR
								}
							}
						}
						579 = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = CAR
									is_subject_of = CAR
								}
							}
						}
						1029 = {
							owner = {
								OR = {
									original_tag = CAR
									is_subject_of = CAR
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					FOP = {
						has_country_flag = car_formable
					}
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 30
		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				release = FOP
				add_political_power = 75
				FOP = {
					load_focus_tree = generic_focus
					set_capital = {
						state = 507
					}
					### Leader
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Juan Domingo Peron"
						desc = "POLITICS_DOMINGO_PERON_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/ARG/Portrait_Argentine_Domingo_Peron.png"
						expire = "1.1.1"
						ideology = absolute_monarchy_subtype
						traits = {
						}
					}
					### Politics
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 10
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 10
						social_conservative = 20
						authoritarian_democrat = 10
						paternal_autocrat = 40
						national_populist = 10
					}
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = paternal_autocrat
						long_name = "Real Audienca de Araucania y Patagonia"
						name = "Real Audienca de Araucania y Patagonia"
					}
					CAR = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = FOP
							autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
						}
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = car_formable
					set_cosmetic_tag = CAR_VICEROY_PATAGONIA
				}
				FOP = {
					every_core_state = {
						remove_core_of = FOP
					}
					270 = {
						add_core_of = FOP
					}
					507 = {
						add_core_of = FOP
					}
					512 = {
						add_core_of = FOP
					}
					579 = {
						add_core_of = FOP
					}
					1029 = {
						add_core_of = FOP
					}
					FOP = {
						every_core_state = {
							limit = {
								AND = {
									NOT = {
										is_core_of = CAR
									}
									OR = {
										is_owned_by = CAR
										OWNER = {
											is_subject_of = CAR
										}
									}
								}
							}
							transfer_state_to = FOP
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		days_remove = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 60
		}
	}
